Method: 将神经策略嵌入已知可微模拟器，用平滑函数近似替代硬约束，利用伴随方法在一次反向传播中精确计算目标函数对所有策略参数和所有输入的梯度，敏感性计算成本仅相当于一次反向传播。

Result: 天然气存储域训练不到1分钟即可获得365条远期曲线敏感性；养老金管理域敏感性计算速度比bump-and-revalue快6.5-200倍；制药制造域在74.5毫秒内通过5次伴随传播获得20个ICH Q8监管敏感性。

Conclusion: SNAPO实现了训练与敏感性计算的一体化，在保持训练效率的同时，以极低成本提供大量精确敏感性，适用于需要快速决策和风险管理的实际序贯决策问题。

Abstract: Many real-world problems require sequential decisions under uncertainty: when to inject or withdraw gas from storage, how to rebalance a pension portfolio each month, what temperature profile to run through a pharmaceutical reactor chain. Dynamic programming solves small instances exactly but scales exponentially in state dimensions. Black-box reinforcement learning handles high-dimensional states but trains slowly and produces no sensitivities. We introduce SNAPO (Smooth Neural Adjoint Policy Optimization), a framework that embeds a neural policy inside a known, differentiable simulator, replaces hard constraints with smooth approximations, and computes exact gradients of the objective with respect to all policy parameters and all inputs in a single adjoint pass. We demonstrate SNAPO on three domains: natural gas storage (training in under a minute, 365 forward curve sensitivities at no additional cost per sensitivity), pension fund asset-liability management (6.5x-200x sensitivity speedup over bump-and-revalue, scaling with the number of risk factors), and pharmaceutical manufacturing (cross-unit sensitivities through a 4-unit process chain, with 20 ICH Q8 regulatory sensitivities from 5 adjoint passes in 74.5 milliseconds). All sensitivities are produced by the same backward pass that trains the policy, at a cost proportional to one reverse pass regardless of how many sensitivities are computed.

### [205] [Directional Consistency as a Complementary Optimization Signal: The GONO Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06575)
*Victor Daniel Gera*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现深度学习优化中存在方向对齐与损失收敛可解耦的现象，并提出GONO优化器，通过动态调整动量系数以利用梯度方向的一致性信号，理论保证收敛速率，实验验证有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有优化器（Adam、SGD、RMSprop）缺乏利用梯度方向时间一致性的显式机制，依赖基于幅度的信号无法区分平台、鞍点与真正收敛，导致方向对齐与损失收敛可能解耦。

Method: 提出GONO（Gradient-Oriented Norm-Adaptive Optimizer），基于连续梯度余弦相似度cc_t动态调整Adam的动量系数β₁：方向一致时放大动量，振荡时抑制动量。理论证明O(1/√T)收敛率，无信息时退化回Adam。

Result: cc_t在振荡检测上F1=1.00（梯度范数仅0.45）；GONO在MNIST（98.15%）、CIFAR-10（43.14%）、ResNet-18（75.44%）上保持与AdamW竞争力。

Conclusion: 方向对齐是一个有理论依据且实践可行的优化信号，GONO验证了该信号的有效性。

Abstract: We identify and formalize an underexplored phenomenon in deep learning optimization: directional alignment and loss convergence can be decoupled. An optimizer can exhibit near-perfect directional consistency (cc_t -> 1, measured via consecutive gradient cosine similarity) while the loss remains high or decreases slowly. This observation reveals that existing optimizers such as Adam, SGD, and RMSprop lack explicit mechanisms to exploit temporal consistency in gradient directions, relying instead on magnitude-based signals that fail to distinguish plateaus, saddle points, and genuine convergence. Motivated by this, we introduce GONO (Gradient-Oriented Norm-Adaptive Optimizer), which adapts Adam's momentum coefficient beta_1 based on cc_t: amplifying momentum under directional consistency and suppressing it during oscillation. We prove GONO matches Adam's O(1/sqrt(T)) convergence rate and reduces exactly to Adam when the signal is uninformative. Empirically, cc_t achieves oscillation detection with F1=1.00 (vs. 0.45 for gradient norm), and GONO remains competitive with AdamW on MNIST (98.15%), CIFAR-10 (43.14%), and ResNet-18 (75.44%), establishing directional alignment as a theoretically grounded, practically actionable optimization signal. Code: https://github.com/victordaniel/gono-optimizer

</details>

*Xiaoguang Guo,Zehong Wang,Ziming Li,Shawn Spitzel,Soonwoo Kwon,Tianyi Ma,Yanfang Ye,Chuxu Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了GRL-Safety，一个多轴安全评估基准，用于系统评估图表示学习方法在五类安全维度（鲁棒性、OOD泛化、类别不平衡、公平性、可解释性）上的表现，揭示了表示设计与压力因素的交互作用、基础模型时代方法的轴特定优势以及现有方法的能力缺口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图表示学习评估主要关注干净迁移、自适应和任务覆盖，但忽略了部署压力（如图信号扰动、图上下文变化、标签支持不足、结构组偏移、预测证据问题）对方法可靠性的影响，缺乏系统的多维度安全评估。

Method: 构建GRL-Safety基准，在标准化评估条件下对12种代表性方法（涵盖拓扑嵌入、监督GNN、自监督图模型、图基础模型）在25个图数据集上进行评估，覆盖五个安全轴（腐败鲁棒性、OOD泛化、类别不平衡、公平性、可解释性），按轴和子条件分别报告而非单一聚合分数，同时保留方法原生自适应能力。

Result: 得到三大跨轴洞察：(1) 安全行为由表示设计与压力因素的交互决定，而非仅由方法家族决定；(2) 基础模型时代方法表现出轴特定优势而非全面安全主导；(3) 多个部署场景即使对最佳方法仍具挑战性，存在能力缺口。

Conclusion: GRL-Safety揭示了当前图表示学习在部署安全性方面的系统性不足，为未来研究提供了明确的方向：需要超越模型选择的新的鲁棒性、自适应或训练目标设计。

Abstract: Graph representation learning (GRL) has evolved from topology-only graph embeddings to task-specific supervised GNNs, and more recently to reusable representations and graph foundation models (GFMs). However, existing evaluations mainly measure clean transfer, adaptation, and task coverage. It remains unclear whether GRL methods stay reliable when deployment stresses affect graph signals, graph contexts, label support, structural groups, or predictive evidence. We introduce GRL-Safety, a multi-axis safety evaluation benchmark for GRL. GRL-Safety evaluates twelve representative methods, spanning topology-only embedding methods, supervised GNNs, self-supervised graph models, and GFMs, on twenty-five graph datasets under standardized evaluation conditions while preserving method-native adaptation. The evaluation covers five safety axes: corruption robustness, OOD generalization, class imbalance, fairness, and interpretation, with per-axis and sub-condition reporting rather than a single aggregate score. Our analysis yields three cross-axis insights that can inspire future research. First, safety behavior is shaped by the interaction between representation design and the stressed graph factor, rather than by method family alone. Second, foundation-era methods show axis-specific strengths rather than broad safety dominance. Third, several deployment regimes remain difficult even for the best evaluated method, revealing capability gaps that require new robustness, adaptation, or training objectives beyond model selection. The benchmark, evaluation protocols, and code are available at: https://github.com/GXG-CS/GRL-Safety.

### [207] [Distributionally-Robust Learning to Optimize](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06585)
*Vinit Ranjan,Jisun Park,Bartolomeo Stellato*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种分布鲁棒的方法来学习凸优化中一阶方法的超参数。通过最小化Wasserstein分布鲁棒版本的性能估计问题(PEP)，统一了经典的学习优化(L2O)和最坏情况最优算法设计。在二次无约束最小化、LASSO和线性规划基准测试中，学习到的算法具有可证明的鲁棒性，优于最坏情况最优和普通L2O基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的学习优化(L2O)方法在训练分布上表现良好，但缺乏对分布偏移的鲁棒性保证；而最坏情况最优算法虽具有稳健性保证，但在典型实例上性能保守。本文旨在弥合两者之间的差距，提出一个统一框架，同时获得数据驱动的高效性和分布鲁棒的保证。

Method: 提出分布鲁棒性能估计问题(PEP)框架。在给定问题实例数据集上，最小化关于算法参数（如步长）的Wasserstein分布鲁棒版本PEP。鲁棒半径为零时退化为经典L2O，半径增大时恢复为最坏情况最优PEP设计。通过随机梯度下降求解，每一步对内部半定规划的解进行微分。

Result: 证明了高概率界限：学习算法的真实风险不超过样本内L2O最优值加上一个随样本量缩减的松弛项，且不劣于最坏情况PEP界。在无约束二次最小化、LASSO和线性规划基准测试上，学习算法具有可证明的鲁棒性，在样本外表现优于最坏情况最优和普通L2O基线。

Conclusion: 该框架成功统一了学习优化和最坏情况最优算法设计两种范式，提供了一种兼具数据驱动高效性和分布鲁棒保证的算法超参数学习方法。

Abstract: We propose a distributionally robust approach to learning hyperparameters for first-order methods in convex optimization. Given a dataset of problem instances, we minimize a Wasserstein distributionally robust version of the performance estimation problem (PEP) over algorithm parameters such as step sizes. Our framework unifies two extremes: as the robustness radius vanishes, we recover classical learning to optimize (L2O); as it grows, we recover worst-case optimal algorithm design via PEP. We solve the resulting problem with stochastic gradient descent, differentiating through the solution of an inner semidefinite program at each step. We prove high-probability bounds showing that the true risk of the learned algorithm is at most the in-sample L2O optimum plus a slack that shrinks with the sample size, and is no worse than the worst-case PEP bound. On unconstrained quadratic minimization, LASSO, and linear programming benchmarks, our learned algorithms achieve strong out-of-sample performance with certifiable robustness, outperforming both worst-case optimal and vanilla L2O baselines.

### [208] [Towards Metric-Faithful Neural Graph Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06588)
*Jyotirmaya Shivottam,Subhankar Mishra*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文构建了连接编码器几何结构与神经图编辑距离（GED）估计质量的理论框架，证明了双Lipschitz编码器可提升GED预测和排序性能，并通过FSW-GNN作为即插即用模块在多个基准上验证了有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管神经图匹配架构在GED估计上取得了显著进展，但编码器几何结构在其中的作用仍缺乏理论理解。

Method: 1) 建立理论框架，分析图级双Lipschitz编码器和节点级双Lipschitz几何对两类GED估计器（图相似性预测器和对齐方法）的影响；2) 提出FSW-GNN作为双Lipschitz、WL等价的编码器，作为即插即用替代模块。

Abstract: Graph Edit Distance (GED) is a fundamental, albeit NP-hard, metric for structural graph similarity. Recent neural graph matching architectures approximate GED by first encoding graphs with a Graph Neural Network (GNN) and then applying either a graph-level regression head or a matching-based alignment module. Despite substantial architectural progress, the role of encoder geometry in neural GED estimation remains poorly understood. In this paper, we develop a theoretical framework that connects encoder geometry to GED estimation quality for two broad classes of neural GED estimators: graph similarity predictors and alignment-based methods. On fixed graph collections, where the doubly-stochastic metric $d_{\mathrm{DS}}$ is comparable to GED, we show that graph-level bi-Lipschitz encoders yield controlled GED surrogates and improved ranking stability; for matching-based estimators, node-level bi-Lipschitz geometry propagates to encoder-induced alignment costs and the resulting optimized alignment objective. We instantiate this perspective using FSW-GNN, a bi-Lipschitz WL-equivalent encoder, as a drop-in replacement in representative neural GED architectures. Across representative baselines and benchmark datasets, the resulting geometry-aware variants significantly improve GED prediction and ranking metrics. A faithfulness case study of untrained encoders, together with ablations and transfer experiments, supports the view that these gains arise from improved representation geometry, positioning encoder geometry as a useful design principle for neural graph matching.

### [209] [Weight-Decay Turns Transformer Loss Landscapes Villani: Functional-Analytic Foundations for Optimization and Generalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06599)
*Abhijit Das,Sayantan Dutta*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文首次从泛函分析角度严格刻画了带权重衰减的Transformer损失函数满足Villani强制能量函数条件，推导了对数Sobolev和Poincaré常数，并通过GPT-Neo-125M实验验证了理论预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 权重衰减在大型语言模型中广泛使用，但其对Transformer损失景观的理论作用尚不明确，缺乏严格的泛函分析刻画。

Method: 证明正则化损失函数满足Villani强制能量函数的四个条件（无限可微、至少二次增长、高斯可积尾部、微分增长条件），推导显式对数Sobolev和Poincaré常数，提出可扩展的Villani诊断量Ψ_s并通过Hutchinson迹估计高效计算。

Result: 在GPT-Neo-125M模型上，Penn Treebank和WikiText-103数据集实验验证了Ψ_s的二次增长、Hessian谱膨胀和指数收敛行为，与对数Sobolev分析一致。

Conclusion: 权重衰减不仅经验上改善泛化，还为快速Langevin混合和曲率感知优化建立了数学条件，连接了正则化强度、模型维度与收敛保证之间的理论关系。

Abstract: Weight decay is widely used as a regularizer in large language models, yet its precise role in shaping Transformer loss landscapes remains theoretically underexplored. This paper provides the first rigorous functional-analytic characterization of the standard Transformer objective--cross-entropy loss with $L^2$ regularization--by proving it satisfies Villani's criteria for coercive energy functions. Specifically, we show that the regularized loss $\mathcal{F}$ is infinitely differentiable, grows at least quadratically, has Gaussian-integrable tails, and satisfies the differential growth condition $-Δ\mathcal{F} + \tfrac{1}{s}\|\nabla\mathcal{F}\|^{2} \to \infty$ as $\|θ\| \to \infty$ for all $s>0$. From this structure, we derive explicit log-Sobolev and Poincaré constants $C_{\mathrm{LS}} \leq λ^{-1} + d/λ^{2}$, linking the regularization strength $λ$ and model dimension $d$ to finite-time convergence guarantees for noisy stochastic gradient descent and PAC-Bayesian generalization bounds that tighten with increasing $λ$. To validate our theory, we introduce a scalable Villani diagnostic $Ψ_s(θ) = -Δ\mathcal{F} + s^{-1}\|\nabla \mathcal{F}\|^2$ and estimate it efficiently using Hutchinson trace probes in models with over 100M parameters. Experiments on GPT-Neo-125M across Penn Treebank and WikiText-103 confirm the predicted quadratic growth of $Ψ_s$, spectral inflation of the Hessian, and exponential convergence behavior consistent with our log-Sobolev analysis. These results demonstrate that weight decay not only improves generalization empirically but also establishes the mathematical conditions required for fast Langevin mixing and theoretically grounded curvature-aware optimization in deep learning.

### [210] [How Many Iterations to Jailbreak? Dynamic Budget Allocation for Multi-Turn LLM Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06605)
*Shai Feldman,Yaniv Romano*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出DAPRO框架，首个在理论上有效的动态预算分配方法，用于在多轮LLM交互中为事件发生时间构建可靠的下界预测区间，在满足预算约束的同时提供无分布假设的有限样本覆盖保证，并在多个任务上优于静态基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多轮对话场景下评估LLM性能计算开销大，关键事件（如越狱、任务完成）往往在多次交互后才出现且可能稀有。现有的共形生存分析方法采用静态预算分配，在多轮设定下效率低下。

Method: 提出DAPRO (Dynamic Allocation via PRojected Optimization) 框架，一种动态预算分配方法，用于在多轮LLM交互中为事件发生时间构建下界预测区间；理论上证明其满足预算约束并提供无分布假设、有限样本的覆盖保证，且无需条件独立性假设；创新性地推导出基于平均删失权重的平方根的更紧覆盖界。

Result: 在Agent任务成功、对抗性越狱、有毒内容生成和RAG幻觉等多个任务上，使用Llama 3.1和Qwen 2.5等LLM的全面实验表明，DAPRO在满足预算约束的同时，始终实现更接近名义覆盖水平的覆盖率且方差低于静态基线方法。

Conclusion: DAPRO为多轮LLM交互中的时间-事件预测提供了首个有效的动态预算分配框架，具有更紧的理论保证和更好的实证性能，同时可用于在有限计算资源下获得无偏、低方差的人口级评估指标估计。

Abstract: Evaluating and predicting the performance of large language models (LLMs) in multi-turn conversational settings is critical yet computationally expensive; key events -- e.g., jailbreaks or successful task completion by an agent -- often emerge only after repeated interactions. These events might be rare, and under any feasible computational budget, remain unobserved.
  Recent conformal survival frameworks construct reliable lower predictive bounds (LPBs) on the number of iterations to trigger the event of interest, but rely on static budget allocation that is inefficient in multi-turn setups. To address this, we introduce \emph{Dynamic Allocation via PRojected Optimization} (DAPRO), the first theoretically valid dynamic budget allocation framework for bounding the time-to-event in multi-turn LLM interactions.
  We prove that DAPRO satisfies the budget constraint and provides distribution-free, finite-sample coverage guarantees without requiring the conditional independence between censoring and event times assumed by prior conformal survival approaches.
  A key theoretical contribution is a novel coverage bound that scales with the square root of the mean censoring weight rather than the worst-case weight, yielding provably tighter guarantees than prior work. Furthermore, DAPRO can be employed to obtain unbiased, low-variance estimates of population-level evaluation metrics, such as the jailbreak rate, under limited computing resources.
  Comprehensive experiments across agentic task success, adversarial jailbreaks, toxic content generation, and RAG hallucinations using LLMs such as Llama 3.1 and Qwen 2.5 demonstrate that DAPRO consistently achieves coverage closer to the nominal level with lower variance than static baselines, while satisfying the budget constraint.

Abstract: Transformers have demonstrated remarkable in-context learning (ICL) capabilities. In this work, we investigate how transformers with softmax attention perform in-context learning on linear classification data. We first construct a class of multi-layer transformers that can perform in-context logistic regression, with each layer exactly performing one step of normalized gradient descent on an in-context loss. Then, we show that our constructed transformer can be obtained through (i) training a single self-attention layer supervised by one-step gradient descent, and (ii) recurrently applying the trained layer to obtain a looped model. ### [212] [SoftSAE: Dynamic Top-K Selection for Adaptive Sparse Autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06610)
*Jakub Stępień,Marcin Mazur,Jacek Tabor,Przemysław Spurek*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SoftSAE提出一种动态Top-K稀疏自编码器，通过可微分的Soft Top-K算子让模型根据输入复杂度自适应调整活跃特征数量，解决了固定稀疏度（K）无法适应真实数据局部内在维度变化的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有TopK SAE等架构使用固定的稀疏度K，对所有输入强制激活相同数量的特征，忽略了真实数据流形上局部内在维度的变化——简单输入需要少量特征，复杂输入需要更多特征，固定K会导致简单输入引入噪声或复杂输入丢失重要结构。

Method: 提出SoftSAE，引入可微分的Soft Top-K算子，使模型能够根据输入复杂度学习依赖输入的稀疏度k，实现动态调整活跃特征数量。

Result: 实验结果表明SoftSAE不仅能发现有意义的特征，还能为每个概念选择正确数量的特征。

Conclusion: 动态稀疏选择机制能更好地匹配数据结构，解释长度能反映输入信息量，相比固定稀疏度方法更具灵活性和适应性。

Abstract: Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) have become an important tool in mechanistic interpretability, helping to analyze internal representations in both Large Language Models (LLMs) and Vision Transformers (ViTs). By decomposing polysemantic activations into sparse sets of monosemantic features, SAEs aim to translate neural network computations into human-understandable concepts. However, common architectures such as TopK SAEs rely on a fixed sparsity level. They enforce the same number of active features (K) across all inputs, ignoring the varying complexity of real-world data. Natural data often lies on manifolds with varying local intrinsic dimensionality, meaning the number of relevant factors can change significantly across samples. This suggests that a fixed sparsity level is not optimal. Simple inputs may require only a few features, while more complex ones need more expressive representations. Using a constant K can therefore introduce noise in simple cases or miss important structure in more complex ones. To address this issue, we propose SoftSAE, a sparse autoencoder with a Dynamic Top-K selection mechanism. Our method uses a differentiable Soft Top-K operator to learn an input-dependent sparsity level k. This allows the model to adjust the number of active features based on the complexity of each input. As a result, the representation better matches the structure of the data, and the explanation length reflects the amount of information in the input. Experimental results confirm that SoftSAE not only finds meaningful features, but also selects the right number of features for each concept. The source code is available at: https://anonymous.4open.science/r/SoftSAE-8F71/.

</details>


### [213] [The Structural Origin of Attention Sink: Variance Discrepancy, Super Neurons, and Dimension Disparity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06611)
*Siquan Li,Kaiqi Jiang,Jiacheng Sun,Tianyang Hu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了LLM中注意力汇聚现象的机制根源：自注意力中的值聚合过程导致系统性方差差异，而FFN层中超级神经元的激活会进一步放大这种差异，迫使模型形成注意力汇聚作为结构性锚点。通过两种干预实验验证了因果链，并提出head-wise RMSNorm架构改进来稳定训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管注意力汇聚现象在LLM中普遍存在，但其结构起源尚不明确，本文旨在提供该现象的机理解释。

Method: 通过理论分析追溯注意力汇聚到自注意力中的值聚合过程引起的方差差异，并揭示FFN层中超级神经元对此差异的放大作用。通过注意力掩码修改和特定token表征方差放大两种干预实验验证因果链，最后提出head-wise RMSNorm架构改进。

Result: 两种干预实验成功在任意位置复现了注意力汇聚现象；head-wise RMSNorm在预训练中恢复了各位置间的统计对等性，显著加速了收敛。

Conclusion: 注意力汇聚的结构根源在于自注意力值聚合与FFN超级神经元激活共同导致的方差差异，对该机制的深入理解为系统性控制注意力汇聚的形成提供了基础。

Abstract: Despite the prevalence of the attention sink phenomenon in Large Language Models (LLMs), where initial tokens disproportionately monopolize attention scores, its structural origins remain elusive. This work provides a \textit{mechanistic explanation} for this phenomenon. First, we trace its root to the value aggregation process inherent in self-attention, which induces a systematic variance discrepancy. We further demonstrate that this discrepancy is drastically amplified by the activation of super neurons within Feed-Forward Network (FFN) layers. Specifically, the channel-sparse down-projections trigger a dimension disparity of the first-token representation, necessitating the formation of attention sinks as a structural anchor. Then, we validate this causal chain through two controlled interventions: (i) isolating the aggregation effect via attention mask modifications and (ii) amplifying the variance of targeted token representations. Both interventions can replicate attention sinks at arbitrary positions. Our mechanistic understanding offers a foundation for the systematic control of sink formation. Finally, as a proof of concept, we propose \textit{head-wise RMSNorm}, an architectural modification that stabilizes value aggregation outputs during pre-training. Our experiments demonstrate that restoring statistical parity across positions significantly accelerates convergence.

### [214] [Online Bayesian Calibration under Gradual and Abrupt System Changes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06612)
*Yang Xu,Chiwoo Park*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出贝叶斯递归投影校准（BRPC）框架，用于流式数据下存在模拟器失配和非平稳性的在线贝叶斯校准。BRPC将投影校准扩展到在线场景，通过分离无差异粒子更新和条件高斯过程差异更新保持可辨识性，并结合重启机制处理突变，在理论和实验上均优于滑动窗口贝叶斯校准和数据同化基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典贝叶斯校准存在参数-差异混杂问题，且作为离线过程假设数据平稳生成，无法适用于数字孪生中系统随时间演化、存在渐进漂移和突变的情况。现有数据同化方法虽能顺序更新，但未显式建模系统偏差，在突变下效果不佳。

Method: BRPC框架包含两个核心组件：(1) 无差异粒子滤波用于校准参数更新，确保可辨识性；(2) 条件高斯过程用于差异函数的在线更新，实现偏差感知的自适应。为处理突变，BRPC集成重启机制，检测系统状态变化并重置校准过程。

Result: 在合成数据和植物模拟基准上的实验表明，BRPC在渐进变化下提高了校准精度；重启增强的BRPC在突变下进一步提升了鲁棒性和预测性能，优于滑动窗口贝叶斯校准和数据同化基线。

Conclusion: BRPC为数字孪生中的在线贝叶斯校准提供了理论基础和有效方法，同时具备渐进变化跟踪和突变检测的理论保证。

Abstract: Bayesian model calibration is central to digital twins and computer experiments, as it aligns model outputs with field observations by estimating calibration parameters and correcting systematic model bias. Classical Bayesian calibration introduces latent parameters and a discrepancy function to model bias, but suffers from parameter--discrepancy confounding and is typically formulated as an offline procedure under a stationary data-generating assumption. These limitations are restrictive in modern digital twin applications, where systems evolve over time and may exhibit gradual drift and abrupt regime shifts. While data assimilation methods enable sequential updates, they generally do not explicitly model systematic bias and are less effective under abrupt changes. We propose Bayesian Recursive Projected Calibration (BRPC), an online Bayesian calibration framework for streaming data under simulator mismatch and nonstationarity. BRPC extends projected calibration to the online setting by separating a discrepancy-free particle update for calibration parameters from a conditional Gaussian process update for discrepancy, preserving identifiability while enabling bias-aware adaptation under gradual system evolution. To handle abrupt changes, BRPC is integrated with restart mechanisms that detect regime shifts and reset the calibration process. We establish theoretical guarantees for both components, including tracking performance under gradual evolution and false-alarm and detection behavior for restart mechanisms. Empirical studies on synthetic and plant-simulation benchmarks show that BRPC improves calibration accuracy under gradual changes, while restart-augmented BRPC further improves robustness and predictive performance under abrupt regime shifts compared to sliding-window Bayesian calibration and data assimilation baselines.

### [217] [Optimizer-Model Consistency: Full Finetuning with the Same Optimizer as Pretraining Forgets Less](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06654)
*Yuxing Liu,Jianyu Wang,Tong Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文发现监督微调（SFT）阶段使用与预训练相同的优化器（即优化器-模型一致性）能实现更好的学习-遗忘权衡，即遗忘更少且在新任务上表现相当或更好。通过实验和理论分析，揭示了优化器通过正则化效应塑造模型激活分布，而一致的优化器产生的权重更新结构有助于保留预训练知识。同时对比了Muon和AdamW，发现Muon在推理任务微调中表现较差，因其倾向于死记硬背而非模式习得。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究监督微调阶段优化器选择对模型性能（特别是学习新知识与遗忘预训练知识之间的权衡）的影响，并提出优化器-模型一致性现象。

Method: 通过控制实验和理论分析，研究不同优化器对模型激活分布的正则化效应，分析权重更新结构与知识保留的关系，并通过合成语言模型实验对比Muon与AdamW在微调中的表现差异。

Result: 1) 优化器通过正则化效应塑造模型激活分布，影响预训练检查点周围的损失景观；2) 为降低遗忘，SFT中权重更新需遵循特定结构，使用相同优化器可获得该结构；3) Muon在推理任务微调中表现差于AdamW，因其强死记硬背倾向不利于小样本模式习得。

Conclusion: 优化器-模型一致性是提升SFT阶段学习-遗忘权衡的重要因素，不同优化器（如Muon与AdamW）在微调中的表现差异源于其内在的正则化效应和记忆倾向差异。

Abstract: Optimizers play an important role in both pretraining and finetuning stages when training large language models (LLMs). In this paper, we present an observation that full finetuning with the same optimizer as in pretraining achieves a better learning-forgetting tradeoff, i.e., forgetting less while achieving the same or better performance on the new task, than other optimizers and, possibly surprisingly, LoRA, during the supervised finetuning (SFT) stage. We term this phenomenon optimizer-model consistency. To better understand it, through controlled experiments and theoretical analysis, we show that: 1) optimizers can shape the models by having regularization effects on the activations, leading to different landscapes around the pretrained checkpoints; 2) in response to this regularization effect, the weight update in SFT should follow some specific structures to lower forgetting of the knowledge learned in pretraining, which can be obtained by using the same optimizer. Moreover, we specifically compare Muon and AdamW when they are employed throughout the pretraining and SFT stages and find that Muon performs worse when finetuned for reasoning tasks. With a synthetic language modeling experiment, we demonstrate that this can come from Muon's strong tendency towards rote memorization, which may hurt pattern acquisition with a small amount of data, as for SFT.

</details>


### [218] [UniPool: A Globally Shared Expert Pool for Mixture-of-Experts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06665)
*Minbin Huang,Han Shi,Chuanyang Zheng,Yimeng Wu,Guoxuan Chen,Xintong Yu,Yichun Yin,Hong Cheng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: UniPool提出了一种共享专家池的MoE架构，替代传统每层独立专家集合的设计，通过全局专家预算、池级辅助损失和NormRouter实现稳定训练。在多个模型尺度上，UniPool相比标准MoE在更少的专家参数下取得更优的验证损失和困惑度，表明专家参数无需随深度线性增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统MoE架构中每层独立拥有专家集合，导致深度扩展时专家参数线性增长。研究发现深层路由存在冗余（随机路由仅带来1.0-1.6点的精度下降），因此希望打破每层独占专家的设计，实现专家容量的全局共享与更高效分配。

Method: 提出UniPool架构：将各层独立的专家集合替换为全局共享的单一专家池，各层使用独立的路由器访问该池；引入池级辅助损失以平衡专家利用率；采用NormRouter实现稀疏且尺度稳定的路由。

Result: 在182M至978M五个尺度上训练30B tokens，UniPool持续优于标准MoE基线，验证损失最多降低0.0386。使用仅41.6%-66.7%专家参数预算的缩减版UniPool即可匹配或超越标准MoE性能，表明专家参数可亚线性增长。

Conclusion: 共享池设计打破了专家参数随深度线性增长的约束，使专家容量成为显式的超参数，实现了更高效有效的MoE架构，且能与细粒度专家分解兼容。

Abstract: Modern Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures allocate expert capacity through a rigid per-layer rule: each transformer layer owns a separate expert set. This convention couples depth scaling with linear expert-parameter growth and assumes that every layer needs isolated expert capacity. However, recent analyses and our routing probe challenge this allocation rule: replacing a deeper layer's learned top-k router with uniform random routing drops downstream accuracy by only 1.0-1.6 points across multiple production MoE models. Motivated by this redundancy, we propose UniPool, an MoE architecture that treats expert capacity as a global architectural budget by replacing per-layer expert ownership with a single shared pool accessed by independent per-layer routers. To enable stable and balanced training under sharing, we introduce a pool-level auxiliary loss that balances expert utilization across the entire pool, and adopt NormRouter to provide sparse and scale-stable routing into the shared expert pool. Across five LLaMA-architecture model scales (182M, 469M, 650M, 830M, and 978M parameters) trained on 30B tokens from the Pile, UniPool consistently improves validation loss and perplexity over the matched vanilla MoE baselines. Across these scales, UniPool reduces validation loss by up to 0.0386 relative to vanilla MoE. Beyond raw loss improvement, our results identify pool size as an explicit depth-scaling hyperparameter: reduced-pool UniPool variants using only 41.6%-66.7% of the vanilla expert-parameter budget match or outperform layer-wise MoE at the tested scales. This shows that, under a shared-pool design, expert parameters need not grow linearly with depth; they can grow sublinearly while remaining more efficient and effective than vanilla MoE. Further analysis shows that UniPool's benefits compose with finer-grained expert decomposition.

</details>

### [219] [DADL: A Declarative Description Language for Enterprise Tool Libraries in LLM Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05247)
*Axel Dunkel*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: DADL (Dunkel API Description Language) 是一种声明式YAML格式，用于统一描述REST API的端点、认证、分页、响应整形和访问分类，通过运行时执行层替代传统的每API专用服务器进程，配合固定大小的Code Mode接口，实现企业级工具库的集中化管理和上下文窗口的显著压缩（142倍缩减）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MCP标准在组织规模下存在两个结构性问题：(1) 每个API集成需部署独立服务器进程，带来重复的部署、依赖和凭据管理开销，且大多数服务器仅仅是REST API的薄包装器；(2) 逐工具注册模型导致上下文窗口消耗随目录规模线性增长，实际部署只能暴露组织实际使用API的一小部分。

Method: 提出DADL (Dunkel API Description Language)，一种YAML声明式格式，单个文件即可描述REST API的端点、认证、分页、响应整形和访问分类。运行时执行层在运行时解释DADL文件，无需部署每API服务器进程或生成集成代码。所有工具共享同一运行时，凭据和授权集中管理，目录通过固定大小的Code Mode接口传递给LLM，大小与目录规模无关。

Result: DADL v0.1规范以CC BY-SA 4.0发布；公共注册表包含20个服务的1,833个工具定义。Code Mode将工具广告的上下文成本从约142,000 tokens降至约1,000 tokens，实现142倍缩减；每次搜索和执行的调用成本取决于具体任务。

Conclusion: DADL通过声明式配置和统一运行时，解决了MCP在组织规模下的服务器碎片化和上下文膨胀问题，构建了可版本化、可审计的企业工具库，任何团队均可通过单一认证授权边界扩展、共享和使用API集成。

Abstract: The Model Context Protocol (MCP) is the standard interface between large language model (LLM) agents and external tools. At organizational scale, however, it exposes two structural problems. First, every API integration is shipped as a dedicated server process with its own deployment, dependency tree, and credential handling; recent empirical work shows the overwhelming majority of these servers are thin wrappers around REST APIs. Second, the per-tool registration model causes context window consumption to grow linearly with catalog size, forcing real deployments to expose only a small fraction of the APIs an organization actually uses.
  We present DADL (Dunkel API Description Language), a YAML format describing a REST API's endpoints, authentication, pagination, response shaping, and access classification in a single declarative file. A DADL file is interpreted by an execution layer at runtime; no per-API server process is deployed and no integration code is generated, though the runtime is itself a server. Because all tools share that runtime, credentials and authorization are managed centrally, and the catalog reaches the LLM through a fixed-size Code Mode interface independent of size. The result is an Enterprise Tool Library: a versioned, auditable collection of API integrations any team can extend, share, and consume through one authentication and authorization boundary.
  The DADL v0.1 specification is released under CC BY-SA 4.0, and a public registry contains 1,833 tool definitions across 20 services. On this catalog, Code Mode reduces the context cost of tool advertisement from approximately 142,000 tokens to approximately 1,000, a 142x reduction; the per-call cost of search and execute invocations is additional and depends on the task.

</details>

*Santosh Vasudevan,Velu Natarajan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于AI文档智能的自动化审计交易测试框架，利用Snowflake Document AI从少量标注的PDF对账单中提取结构化数据，并与权威数据源进行大规模对账，实现从抽样测试到全量测试的转变，提升审计覆盖率和持续保证能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统手工抽样审计方式在处理非结构化PDF对账单时效率低下，无法扩展到百万级交易量，亟需一种可规模化、自动化的审计交易测试方法。

Method: 采用Snowflake Document AI，仅需约20份标注文档即可训练模型，从非结构化PDF对账单中提取结构化数据，并与权威源数据集进行自动化对账，通过交互式仪表盘和自动化报告展示结果。

Result: 实现了从抽样测试到全量（总体级）测试的转变，显著提升了审计覆盖率，支持近乎实时的风险识别和持续保证目标。

Conclusion: 基于文档智能和分析驱动的审计框架能够实现可扩展、近实时的风险识别与持续保证，为大规模审计交易测试提供了一种有效的自动化解决方案。

Abstract: Audit transaction testing validates accuracy and completeness of customer-facing statements against internal systems of record. Traditional manual, sample-based review of unstructured PDF statements is labor-intensive and does not scale to millions of transactions. This paper presents an automated framework for large-scale audit transaction testing using AI-based document intelligence. The solution leverages Snowflake Document AI to extract structured data from unstructured PDF statements using a small labeled corpus (approximately 20 documents). Extracted data are reconciled against authoritative source-of-truth datasets to identify discrepancies at scale. Results are surfaced through interactive dashboards and automated reports. The framework enables population-level testing rather than sampling-based approaches, improving audit coverage and supporting continuous assurance objectives. Recent advances in document intelligence and analytics-driven audit frameworks enable scalable, near real-time risk identification and continuous assurance.

### [221] [PARNESS: A Paper Harness for End-to-End Automated Scientific Research with Dynamic Workflows, Full-Text Indexing, and Cross-Run Knowledge Accumulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05258)
*Yuchen Wang,Zhongzhi Luan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: PARNESS 是一个开源框架，通过四层设计（DAG内核解耦调度、全文PDF解析、知识图谱索引、编码Agent扩展）克服现有LLM科研自动化系统的流程僵化问题，实现跨学科的动态科研工作流编排与跨运行知识持久化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自主研究系统（AI-Scientist、PaperOrchestra等）在框架层面固定了单一的控制流形状（线性管线、状态机、单Agent循环等），但科研工作流本质上是动态且学科特异的，现有系统的僵化来自五个根源：工作流动态性与学科特异性、跨领域构思受限于LLM上下文、摘要视图不足以代表全文、论文与开源代码库的链接被忽略、缺乏跨运行知识持久化工具。

Method: PARNESS 采用四项设计策略：(i) 薄DAG内核 + 四字段Agent契约，将调度与领域语义解耦，学科工作流可用YAML表达；(ii) 全文PDF解析与文献库子系统，将论文正文、图表索引为类型化对象，并支持优雅地回退到摘要；(iii) 基于论文、想法、实验和代码库的知识图谱索引，支持场景化检索（相似/矛盾/跨领域/反直觉）；(iv) 轻量扩展接口，允许任何现代编码Agent（Claude Code、Cursor等）添加或替换模块。

Result: 据作者称，PARNESS 是首个结合声明式管线、全文PDF与代码库索引、以及跨运行知识持久化的开源系统。代码已开源在GitHub。

Conclusion: 通过DAG调度解耦、全文内容索引、知识图谱检索和Agent扩展机制，PARNESS 解决了现有LLM科研自动化框架流程僵化的根本问题，为跨学科、跨运行、可扩展的自主科研系统提供了新的框架范式。

Abstract: Recent autonomous research systems -- AI-Scientist, PaperOrchestra, AutoSOTA, DeepResearch, InternAgent, ResearchAgent and others -- show LLM agents can ideate, run experiments and write papers, but each fixes a particular control-flow shape (linear pipeline, state machine, single-agent loop, or fixed-recipe skill pack) at the framework level. We argue this rigidity has five roots: (1) workflows are dynamic and discipline-specific (lab work, surveys, simulations, theory all loop differently); (2) ideation is bounded by LLM context and cross-domain ideation needs knowledge a single context cannot hold; (3) summary-only views miss the paper body, yet full-text access is uneven, so the cumulative corpus must do the work; (4) a paper's open-source repository is often the only complete specification of its experimental scheme, but the paper-to-code link is neglected; (5) no tool persists cross-run knowledge retrievably into a finite LLM context.
  We present PARNESS, an open-source framework built on four design moves. (i) A thin DAG kernel with a four-field Agent contract decouples scheduling from domain semantics, so any discipline's loop is expressible as user-editable YAML. (ii) A full-text PDF-parsing and literature-library subsystem indexes paper bodies, figures and tables as typed objects, with graceful abstract-only fall-back. (iii) A knowledge-graph index over papers, ideas, experiments and code repositories, with scenario-typed retrieval (similar / contradictory / cross-domain / counter-intuitive), surfaces a focused slice into each LLM call. (iv) A small extension surface lets any modern coding agent (Claude Code, Cursor, Copilot, OpenCode) add or replace any module. To our knowledge PARNESS is the first open-source system combining declarative pipelines, full-PDF and code-repository indexing, and cross-run knowledge. Source: https://github.com/gtrhythm/PARNESS

</details>


### [222] [Bridging Generation and Training: A Systematic Review of Quality Issues in LLMs for Code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05267)
*Kaifeng He,Xiaojun Zhang,Peiliang Cai,Mingwei Liu,Yanlin Wang,Chong Wang,Kaifeng Huang,Bihuan Chen,Xin Peng,Zibin Zheng*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过系统文献综述（114篇研究），建立了训练数据质量问题与代码生成缺陷之间的因果映射框架，提出了统一的分类法（9维代码质量+代码/非代码数据属性），总结了18种传播机制，并识别出质量保证正从被动过滤转向主动数据治理的趋势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在代码生成中频繁产生缺陷（逻辑错误到安全漏洞），尽管常被视为模型层面问题，但实证表明其根因在于训练语料的质量缺陷。然而，训练数据质量与生成代码质量之间的具体传播机制尚未被系统地映射和理解。

Method: 对114篇主要研究进行系统文献综述，建立统一的分类法（9维生成代码质量+代码/非代码训练数据属性），形式化因果框架描述18种典型传播映射机制，并综合数据、模型和生成生命周期各阶段的检测与缓解技术。

Result: 建立了从训练数据质量到生成代码质量的因果传播映射框架（18种机制），揭示了质量保证方法论正从反应式、基于启发式的后生成过滤转向主动式、数据驱动的治理与闭环修复。

Conclusion: 提出了未来研究方向：通过集成数据策展和持续评估来开发可靠的代码生成LLM，并指出质量保证范式的转变趋势。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) frequently generate defective outputs in code generation tasks, ranging from logical bugs to security vulnerabilities. While these generation failures are often treated as model-level limitations, empirical evidence increasingly traces their root causes to imperfections within the training corpora. Yet, the specific mechanisms linking training data quality issues to generated code quality issues remain largely unmapped. This paper presents a systematic literature review of 114 primary studies to investigate how training data quality issues propagate into code generation. We establish a unified taxonomy that categorizes generated code quality issues across nine dimensions and training data quality issues into code and non-code attributes. Based on this taxonomy, we formalize a causal framework detailing 18 typical propagation mapping mechanisms. Furthermore, we synthesize state-of-the-art detection and mitigation techniques across the data, model, and generation lifecycles. The reviewed literature reveals a clear methodological shift: quality assurance is transitioning from reactive, heuristic-based post-generation filtering toward proactive, data-centric governance and closed-loop repair. Finally, we identify open challenges and outline research directions for developing reliable LLMs for code through integrated data curation and continuous evaluation. Our repository is available at https://github.com/SYSUSELab/From-Data-to-Code.

</details>


### [223] [Mise en Place for Agentic Coding: Deliberate Preparation as Context Engineering Methodology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05400)
*Andrew Zigler*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出"准备工作方法论"(MEP)，通过上下文基础、协作规范和任务分解三阶段，解决AI编码智能体因缺乏上下文导致的系统对齐问题，并在黑客马拉松中验证了该方法能使多智能体并行实现全栈应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前"氛围编码"模式追求实现速度而忽视准备阶段，导致AI智能体因缺乏充分上下文而生成需大量调试和重构的代码，造成开发时间的系统性浪费。作者旨在解决这一对齐问题。

Method: 借鉴烹饪中的"mise en place"理念，提出三阶段准备方法：(1)上下文基础——将领域专长和隐性知识外化为结构化文档；(2)协作规范——通过人机对话生成详细设计工件；(3)任务分解——将规范转换为结构化、感知依赖关系的任务记录。

Result: 在竞争性黑客马拉松中，约两小时的MEP准备使得多个并发AI智能体能够快速并行实现一个全栈教育平台，验证了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 引入"上下文流畅度"作为新兴开发者技能概念，将其与逆向设计和隐性知识外化等既有框架联系，并提出AI辅助软件开发中准备阶段方法的实证研究议程。

Abstract: The rapid adoption of AI coding agents has produced a dominant workflow pattern -- often called "vibe coding" -- that prioritizes speed of implementation over deliberate preparation. We argue that this approach creates a systematic alignment problem: agents that lack sufficient context produce code requiring extensive debugging and refactoring, consuming substantial development time. Drawing on the culinary concept of mise en place (everything in its place; abbreviated MEP), we propose a three-phase preparation methodology for agentic coding: (1) contextual grounding, where domain expertise and tacit knowledge are externalized into structured documents; (2) collaborative specification, where human-agent dialogue produces detailed design artifacts; and (3) task decomposition, where specifications are converted into structured, dependency-aware task records. We report on the application of MEP during a competitive hackathon, where roughly two hours of preparation enabled a rapid parallel implementation of a full-stack educational platform by concurrent AI agents. We introduce the concept of context fluency as an emerging developer skill -- the ability to create rich, structured context that agents can act on -- and connect it to established frameworks in backward design and tacit knowledge externalization. We conclude with a research agenda for empirically validating preparation-phase methodologies in AI-assisted software development.

</details>


### [224] [Is this Build Failure Related to my Patch? An Empirical Study of Unrelated Build Failures in Continuous Integration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05564)
*Andie Huang,Daniel Alencar da Costa,Grant Dick,Mariam El Mezouar*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文研究了Apache开源项目中77,354次CI构建失败，发现开发者平均花费4小时判断构建失败是否与自己的代码推送相关。通过分析371个确认的无关构建失败，提出了一种基于正无标记(PU)学习的方法，利用33个特征预测无关构建失败，在7个Apache项目上达到了0.70-0.88的精确率和0.63-0.97的AUC。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在CI系统并发运行多个构建的场景中，构建失败可能并非由触发它的代码推送引起，开发者需要花费大量时间判断失败是否与自己的更改相关，造成开发效率浪费。

Method: 收集77,354次CI构建失败数据，对371个确认的无关构建失败进行文档分析，提取33个特征（包括CI延迟、重复错误消息、前置评论数量等），构建半监督正无标记(PU)学习模型进行预测。

Result: PU学习模型在7个Apache项目上精确率0.70-0.88，召回率0.30-1.00，F1-score 0.44-0.91，AUC 0.63-0.97。无关测试失败占开发者分类为无关构建失败的20%。

Conclusion: PU学习可以有效帮助开发者识别那些不太可能由当前代码推送引起的构建失败，减少不必要的调试时间。

Abstract: Continuous Integration (CI) systems often run many builds concurrently. In this setting, a legitimate build failure may not be caused by the code push that triggered it. Such unrelated build failures can waste developer effort because developers must determine whether the failure is actionable for their current change. We study 77,354 CI build failures from seven open source Apache projects to understand and predict unrelated build failures. We find that developers spend a median of 4 hours identifying whether a failure is related or unrelated to their push. We also perform a document analysis of 371 confirmed unrelated build failures sampled from 10,316 potentially unrelated failures. The analysis shows that unrelated test failures account for 20% of the cases in which developers classify build failures as unrelated. To predict unrelated build failures, we extract 33 features from issue reports, issue comments, and commits associated with the triggering push. We build semi-supervised Positive and Unlabeled (PU) learning models for seven Apache projects. The models achieve precision from 0.70 to 0.88, recall from 0.30 to 1.00, F1-score from 0.44 to 0.91, and AUC from 0.63 to 0.97. Feature importance analysis shows that CI latency, repeated error messages, and the number of preceding comments are useful indicators of unrelated build failures. These results show that PU learning can help developers identify build failures that are unlikely to be caused by their current push.

</details>


### [225] [An Empirical Study of Proactive Coding Assistants in Real-World Software Development](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05700)
*Lehui Li,Ruixuan Jia,Guo-Ye Yang,Jia Li*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过大规模实证研究发现，基于LLM模拟的开发者行为数据与真实IDE交互数据在行为多样性、时间结构和探索模式上存在显著差距。基于真实数据构建的ProCodeBench基准测试表明，当前方法在真实场景下表现不佳，模拟数据无法替代真实数据，但可在真实微调前作为补充。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有主动式编码助手研究受限于缺乏大规模真实开发者行为数据，多依赖LLM模拟的IDE轨迹数据，但这些模拟数据对真实开发行为的保真度尚不明确，亟需系统性研究两者之间的差距。

Method: 收集1,246名资深行业开发者连续三天的真实IDE交互数据，并构建配对的LLM模拟轨迹进行对比分析；基于真实数据构建ProCodeBench基准，评估多种LLM、检索增强方法和智能体基线在主动意图预测任务上的表现。

Result: 模拟轨迹在行为多样性、时间结构和探索模式上与真实轨迹存在显著差异；当前方法在真实IDE轨迹下表现远未达到可靠水平，基于模拟的评价会高估真实性能；模拟数据无法替代真实数据，但可在真实微调前作为补充。

Conclusion: 真实开发者行为数据对评估和训练主动式编码助手至关重要，模拟数据的盲目使用可能导致对模型实际性能的误判。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based coding assistants have made substantial progress, yet most systems remain reactive, requiring developers to explicitly formulate their needs. Proactive coding assistants aim to infer latent developer intent from integrated development environment (IDE) interactions and repository context, thereby reducing interaction overhead and supporting more seamless assistance. However, research in this direction is limited by the scarcity of large-scale real-world developer behavior data. Existing studies therefore often rely on LLM-simulated IDE traces, whose fidelity to real development behavior remains unclear. In this paper, we investigate this simulation-to-reality gap through a large-scale empirical study. We collect real IDE interaction traces from 1{,}246 experienced industry developers over three consecutive days using a custom Visual Studio Code extension, and construct paired LLM-simulated traces for controlled comparison. Our analysis shows that simulated traces differ substantially from real traces in behavioral diversity, temporal structure, and exploratory patterns. Based on the collected data, we introduce \textbf{ProCodeBench}, a real-world benchmark for proactive intent prediction. Experiments with representative LLMs, retrieval-augmented methods, and agentic baselines show that current approaches remain far from reliable under real IDE traces, suggesting that simulation-based evaluation can overestimate real-world performance. Finally, our training study shows that simulated data cannot replace real data, but can complement it when used before real-world fine-tuning. These findings highlight the importance of real developer behavior data for evaluating and training proactive coding assistants.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: OntoAgent自动分析领域需求描述构建经验本体，在访谈中通过四种操作（ParseUser、ScoreOnto、ReRankOnto、GatePrune）识别相关需求关注点，结合对话上下文生成获取问题。

Abstract: Requirements elicitation interviews are crucial and time-consuming in requirements engineering, but heavily rely on the experience of requirements analysts. Although recent advancements in large language models (LLMs) have created new opportunities to automate this process, existing approaches rely solely on LLMs for free-form chat without taking into account the interview and development experience. That leads to the omission of implicit requirements and redundant questions. Practically, experienced analysts implicitly follow a structured cognitive framework when conducting requirements elicitation. Inspired by this observation, this paper proposes an interview agent named OntoAgent for the elicitation of requirements guided by an experience ontology. OntoAgent automatically analyzes domain-specific requirements descriptions to construct an experience ontology, which organizes requirements concerns into an ontology to support systematic and explainable interviews. During the interview, OntoAgent first performs four operations (i.e., ParseUser, ScoreOnto, ReRankOnto, GatePrune) guided by the ontology to identify the relevant requirement concerns. The selected concern is then combined with the current dialogue context to generate the elicitation question. To validate OntoAgent, we conduct comprehensive quantitative experiments using the widely adopted website application domain. The results show that OntoAgent significantly outperforms existing baselines in both elicitation effectiveness and questioning efficiency, achieving a 33% improvement in IRE and a 21% improvement in TKQR. Ablation studies further validate the contribution of each key design component. In addition, a qualitative user study demonstrates its practical advantages in real-world scenarios. We believe that OntoAgent can also be extended to requirements interview tasks in other domains.

### [227] [On Fixing Insecure AI-Generated Code through Model Fine-Tuning and Prompting Strategies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05867)
*Ali Soltanian Fard Jahromi,Amjed Tahir,Peng Liang,Foutse Khomh*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了针对AI生成代码的安全加固策略，评估了微调和提示工程等方法在多个模型和编程语言上对CWE弱点的缓解效果。结果表明安全改进高度依赖策略和模型，且修复弱点时常引入新的弱点，不存在普适有效的"防弹"解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用微调和提示工程两种方法对模型输出进行精炼，系统评估多种安全加固策略在多个模型和编程语言上对CWE弱点的缓解效果，包括弱点严重性、共现性分析以及修复的副作用评估。

Result: 安全改进高度依赖于具体策略和模型；某些方法能减少特定类别的弱点，但常以引入新弱点为代价；没有任何策略能在所有模型和场景下一致消除弱点。

Conclusion: 当前不存在通用有效的"防弹"解决方案来确保AI生成代码的安全性，安全加固策略存在明显的权衡取舍效应。

Abstract: The security of AI-generated code remains a major obstacle to its widespread adoption. Although code generation models achieve strong performance on functional benchmarks, their outputs frequently contain bugs and security weaknesses that undermine their trustworthiness. Prior work has explored a range of approaches to mitigate security issues in AI-generated code, e.g., using static analysis-guided generation and prompt engineering. However, their effectiveness varies widely across models and settings. This paper presents a systematic investigation of strategies for hardening model-generated code against a list of Common Weakness Enumeration (CWE). We assess the extent to which these strategies improve security across models and programming languages, using fine-tuning and prompting approaches for model output refinement. Beyond the prevalence of security weaknesses, we analyse the severity of identified CWEs, their co-occurrence, and the unintended consequences of remediation (i.e., whether fixing certain weaknesses introduces new weaknesses elsewhere in the same code). Our results show that security improvements are highly strategy- and model-dependent. Although some approaches reduce specific classes of weaknesses, they often introduce new weaknesses as side effects of the fixes. Moreover, no strategy consistently eliminates weaknesses across all models and scenarios, highlighting the absence of a universally effective "bulletproof" solution for secure AI-generated code.

### [228] [Evaluating Non-English Developer Support in Machine Learning for Software Engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05902)

Conclusion: 评估与生成是多语言代码工具面临的关键障碍，人类判断在当前阶段仍不可或缺。

Abstract: Large Language Models are increasingly used in software engineering, but both code generation and its evaluation remain predominantly English-centric. This leaves a major gap in our understanding of how well current tools support multilingual development, where code contains non-English natural language. In this paper, we investigate non-English code comment generation and the reliability of current methods for evaluating such outputs. We evaluate five code LLMs (CodeGemma, CodeLlama, CodeQwen1.5, GraniteCode, and StarCoder2) across five natural languages: Dutch, English, Greek, Polish and Chinese. We further conduct an open-coding study of 12,500 generated comments, from which we derive a publicly released human-annotated dataset and a taxonomy of 26 error types. We use these human annotations, to evaluate the performance of neural metrics, and LLM-as-a-judge pipelines.
  Our findings show that generative performance deteriorates substantially outside English, with linguistic errors increasing by up to 15.1$\times$, alongside frequent incoherent generations and a rise in semantic errors. More critically, we show that detecting errors in non-English comments underperforms. Across classical overlap-based metrics, off-the-shelf neural metrics, extended neural metrics using newer multilingual, language-specific, and code-specific models, and LLM-as-a-judge pipelines, no automatic approach provides reliable and consistent assessment. Neural metrics fail to distinguish correct comments from incorrect outputs or even random noise, and tend to overestimate quality in non-English settings. LLM-as-a-judge methods achieve the highest agreement with human annotations but fail to reliably capture important language-related and semantic errors. Overall, our results show that evaluation and generation are key barriers for multilingual tooling, and that human judgment remains indispensable.

### [229] [Schedule-and-Calibrate: Utility-Guided Multi-Task Reinforcement Learning for Code LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06111)
*Yujia Chen,Yang Ye,Xiao Chu,Yuchi Ma,Cuiyun Gao*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: ASTOR 是一个多任务代码强化学习框架，通过任务效用驱动的分层数据调度和自适应策略优化，在单一 LLM 上实现比任务专用专家模型和现有 MTRL 基线更优的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于可验证奖励的 RL 方法在代码后训练中需要为每个任务部署专用专家模型，成本随任务数量线性增长；而现有的多任务 RL 方法对所有编码任务一视同仁，依赖固定的数据课程和共享优化策略，限制了多任务训练的有效性。

Method: ASTOR 包含两个耦合模块：1) 分层效用路由数据调度模块，基于任务效用分层分配训练预算并优先选择信息量大的提示；2) 自适应效用校准策略优化模块，根据每任务当前训练状态动态缩放 KL 正则化。

Result: 在两种广泛使用的 LLM 和四个代表性编码任务上，ASTOR 在单一模型上全面优于所有任务，比最佳任务专用专家模型提升 9.0%-9.5%，比最强 MTRL 基线提升 7.5%-12.8%。

Conclusion: ASTOR 通过任务效用驱动的协调机制，有效解决了多任务代码 RL 训练中数据调度和策略优化的问题，实现了单一模型在多个编码任务上的超越专家性能。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) with verifiable rewards has proven effective at post-training LLMs for coding, yet deploying separate task-specific specialists incurs costs that scale with the number of tasks, motivating a unified multi-task RL (MTRL) approach. However, existing MTRL methods treat all coding tasks uniformly, relying on fixed data curricula under a shared optimization strategy, ultimately limiting the effectiveness of multi-task training. To address these limitations, we propose ASTOR, a multi-tASk code reinforcement learning framework via uTility-driven coORdination. Centered on task utility, a signal capturing each task learning potential and cross-task synergy, ASTOR comprises two coupled modules: 1) Hierarchical Utility-Routed Data Scheduling module hierarchically allocates training budget and prioritizes informative prompts, steering training toward the most valuable data and 2) Adaptive Utility-Calibrated Policy Optimization module dynamically scales per-task KL regularization, matching update constraints to each tasks current training state. Experiments on two widely-used LLMs across four representative coding tasks demonstrate that ASTOR consistently improves a single model across all tasks, outperforming the best task-specific specialist by 9.0%-9.5% and surpassing the strongest MTRL baseline by 7.5%-12.8%.

### [230] [Breaking, Stale, or Missing? Benchmarking Coding Agents on Project-Level Test Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06125)
*Ye Shang,Quanjun Zhang,Haichuan Hu,Chunrong Fang,Liang Xiao,Zhenyu Chen*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: TEBench是首个项目级别的测试演化基准，包含314个来自Defects4J项目的任务实例，涵盖三种演化类型（测试断裂、测试陈旧、测试缺失）。评估表明，七个配置的识别F1分数集中在45.7%-49.4%，存在性能天花板，且测试陈旧类型最具挑战性（F1约36%），现有方法依赖执行失败信号而缺乏主动语义推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有测试演化基准在方法级别粒度上操作，使用预先配对的输入，绕过了从完整项目中定位受影响测试的任务，且完全排除了编写新测试的需求。缺乏一个项目级别的基准来评估系统在真实场景中自主识别需修改的测试、确定需要新测试的位置并生成相应测试补丁的能力。

Method: 通过四阶段流水线在Defects4J项目上构建TEBench，从10个项目中筛选出314个带有开发者编写ground truth的任务实例。每个实例标注一种或多种演化类型：Test-Breaking（失败测试）、Test-Stale（仍通过但不再有效验证更新行为的测试）、Test-Missing（为引入行为所需的新测试）。评估了跨越三个工业Agent框架（Claude Code、Codex CLI、OpenCode）和六个基础模型的七个配置，以及一个启发式基线。

Result: 所有七个配置的识别F1分数收敛在45.7%到49.4%之间，表明框架和基础模型之间存在共享的性能天花板。Test-Stale是最具挑战性的类型，平均F1约36%，因为配置依赖执行失败信号而缺乏主动语义推理。在更新任务上，配置生成的测试修改具有高度可执行性，但其表面形式与ground truth存在实质性差异。轨迹分析揭示了一个反应式的"执行-失败-修复"循环，该循环对断裂测试有效，但在结构上无法处理陈旧或缺失的测试。

Conclusion: TEBench作为首个项目级测试演化基准，揭示了现有方法在测试陈旧和测试缺失任务上的显著局限性。未来工作需要从当前的"执行-失败-修复"反应式范式转向更具主动性的语义推理方法，以解决测试演化中的全部挑战。基准和排行榜已公开可用。

Abstract: As production code evolves, the test suite must co-evolve to remain effective. Existing benchmarks for test evolution operate at method-level granularity with pre-paired inputs, bypassing the task of locating affected tests from the full project and excluding the need for new tests entirely. We present TEBench, the first project-level benchmark for test evolution. Given a project repository and a code-changing commit, TEBench requires systems to autonomously identify tests requiring modification, determine where new tests are needed, and produce the corresponding test patch. We construct TEBench through a four-stage pipeline over Defects4J projects, curating 314 task instances from 10 projects with developer-written ground truth. Each instance is annotated with one or more of three evolution types: Test-Breaking (tests that fail), Test-Stale (tests that pass but no longer meaningfully validate updated behavior), and Test-Missing (new tests needed for introduced behavior). We evaluate seven configurations spanning three industrial agent frameworks (Claude Code, Codex CLI, OpenCode) and six base models, alongside a heuristic baseline. All seven configurations converge on an identification F1 of 45.7% to 49.4%, revealing a shared performance ceiling across both frameworks and base models. Test-Stale is the most challenging type, averaging F1 around 36%, since configurations rely on execution failure signals and lack proactive semantic reasoning. On the update task, configurations produce highly executable test modifications whose surface form diverges substantially from ground truth. Trajectory analysis reveals a reactive "execute-fail-fix" loop that succeeds for breaking tests but structurally cannot address stale or missing tests. TEBench is available at https://github.com/iSEngLab/TEBench with a leaderboard at https://tebench-leadership.vercel.app.

### [231] [Teaching LLMs Program Semantics via Symbolic Execution Traces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06184)
*Jonas Bayer,Stefan Zetzsche,Olivier Bouissou,Remi Delmas,Michael Tautschnig,Soonho Kong*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出基于SV-COMP 2025的500个C语言验证任务评估框架，发现现有模型在检测违反性质方面存在严重缺陷（尤其随程序长度增加而下降）。通过在开源C代码上运行Soteria符号执行引擎生成形式化验证轨迹，对Qwen3-8B进行持续预训练，仅用约3000条bug轨迹结合思维链推理即可将违规检测提升17个百分点以上，在8B规模上接近甚至超越32B模型。轨迹训练与思维链的协同效应超加性，且改进跨所有五种属性类型泛化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有C程序验证评估中，模型总体准确率高但掩盖了违规检测能力严重不足的问题，尤其对长程序违规检测退化显著。需要弥合这一差距。

Method: 构建500个C验证任务（涵盖内存安全、溢出、终止、可达性、数据竞争五类属性），基于SV-COMP 2025。在通用开源C代码上运行Soteria符号执行引擎生成形式化验证轨迹，用轨迹数据对Qwen3-8B进行持续预训练，并在推理阶段结合思维链推理。

Result: 约3000条bug轨迹+思维链推理使违规检测提升17+个百分点；8B模型在违规检测上超越4倍大的Qwen3-32B（无思考模式），总体准确率接近32B模型；轨迹训练与思维链的协同效应超加性（单独使用均无显著提升）；改进跨所有五种属性类型泛化。

Conclusion: 形式化验证轨迹训练与思维链推理的组合能有效提升LLM在程序验证中违规检测的短板，效果源于轨迹语义而非代码量，且轨迹的整理和格式至关重要。

Abstract: We introduce an evaluation framework of 500 C verification tasks across five property types (memory safety, overflow, termination, reachability, data races) built on SV-COMP 2025, and evaluate 14 models across six families. We find that high overall accuracy masks a critical weakness: while most models reliably confirm properties hold, violation detection varies widely and degrades sharply with program length. To close this gap, we train on formal verification artifacts: running the Soteria symbolic execution engine on generic open-source C code and using the resulting traces for continued pretraining of Qwen3-8B. Just ${\sim}$3,000 bug traces combined with chain-of-thought reasoning at inference time improve violation detection by over 17 percentage points, producing one of the most balanced accuracy profiles among evaluated models. On violation detection, the trained 8B model outperforms the 4$\times$ larger Qwen3-32B without thinking and approaches it in overall accuracy. The interaction between trace training and chain-of-thought is superadditive: neither alone provides meaningful gains, but their combination does. Improvements transfer across all five property types, including ones the training traces do not target. Our 28 configurations confirm the gains stem from trace semantics, not code volume, and that trace curation and format matter.

### [232] [SiblingRepair: Sibling-Based Multi-Hunk Repair with Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06209)
*Xinyu Liu,Jiayu Ren,Yusen Wang,Qi Xin,Xiaoyuan Xie,Jifeng Xuan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: SiblingRepair是一种基于LLM的多hunk自动程序修复技术，专门用于修复代码中具有相似问题的孪生位置。它通过令牌和嵌入匹配搜索语义相似的孪生候选，利用LLM识别与故障相关的孪生，并采用同时修复和迭代修复两种策略生成一致的补丁，在Defects4J和GHRB基准测试中显著优于现有SOTA技术。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发者在实现相关功能时常常在不同代码位置犯相似错误（称为孪生位置），需要一致的修复。现有SOTA技术Hercules在孪生检测和修复方面存在强假设、刚性匹配和模板局限等问题，亟需一种更灵活、准确的方法来识别和修复孪生错误。

Method: SiblingRepair从频谱故障定位识别的可疑位置出发，通过令牌匹配和嵌入匹配搜索语义相关的孪生候选，不局限于故障覆盖或提交历史。然后利用LLM识别与故障相关的孪生，并通过两种互补策略生成一致补丁：(1) 同时修复策略，联合修复多个孪生；(2) 迭代修复策略，逐步分析候选位置构建补丁。最后保留来自多个可疑位置的有效补丁，组合为通用的多hunk补丁。

Result: 在Defects4J和GHRB基准上的评估显示，SiblingRepair显著优于包括Hercules在内的SOTA多hunk修复技术。进一步实验证明了其修复效率、孪生检测和修复组件的有效性，以及LLM数据泄露对结果的有限影响。

Conclusion: SiblingRepair通过结合LLM的语义理解能力和灵活的匹配策略，有效克服了现有孪生修复技术的局限性，推动了自动化孪生修复和通用多hunk修复的发展。

Abstract: Developers often make similar mistakes across code locations implementing related functionalities. These locations, called siblings, share similar issues and require similar fixes. Accurately identifying siblings and consistently repairing them are crucial for automated program repair. Hercules is a SOTA technique designed for sibling repair. However, it is limited by strong assumptions about sibling locations and commit-history availability, rigid AST-based sibling matching, and inflexible template-based patch generation. To address these limitations, we present SiblingRepair, a new LLM-based multi-hunk APR technique specialized for sibling repair. Starting from a suspicious location identified by spectrum-based fault localization, SiblingRepair searches for semantically related sibling candidates using token- and embedding-based code matching, without restricting discovery to failing-test coverage or commit history. It then uses an LLM to identify failure-relevant siblings and generate consistent patches through two complementary strategies: simultaneous repair, which jointly repairs siblings, and iterative repair, which progressively analyzes candidates for patch construction. SiblingRepair further preserves promising patches generated from earlier suspicious locations and combines them into generalized multi-hunk patches. We evaluate SiblingRepair on the Defects4J and GHRB benchmarks. The results show that SiblingRepair substantially outperforms SOTA multi-hunk repair techniques including Hercules. Our evaluation further demonstrates its repair efficiency, the effectiveness of its sibling detection and repair components, and limited impact of the LLM data leakage on the results. Overall, SiblingRepair advances automated sibling and general multi-hunk repair.

</details>


### [233] [Correct Code, Vulnerable Dependencies: A Large Scale Measurement Study of LLM-Specified Library Versions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06279)
*Chengjie Wang,Jingzheng Wu,Xiang Ling,Tianyue Luo,Chen Zhao*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本研究首次大规模测量了LLM生成Python代码中第三方库版本选择的安全与兼容性风险。对10个LLM在1000个编程任务上测试发现：模型倾向于指定版本标识符（6.45%-95.18%），其中36.70%-55.70%的任务包含已知CVE漏洞，62.75%-74.51%为高危或严重等级，72.27%-91.37%的CVE在模型知识截止前已公开。所有模型收敛于相同的高风险版本，静态兼容率仅19.70%-63.20%，动态通过率6.49%-48.62%。外部锚定版本约束可显著降低漏洞暴露和兼容性失败。研究揭示版本选择是LLM开发中一个被忽视的一级风险面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM生成的代码常包含带具体版本号的第三方库导入，这些版本选择可能带来安全和兼容性风险，但此前缺乏系统研究。

Method: 构建PinTrace基准（1000个Stack Overflow编程任务），评估10个LLM的版本指定行为；分析CVE暴露、严重等级、知识截止时间对比；测量静态兼容性和动态通过率；进行归因实验区分版本选择与代码质量问题，并测试外部锚定约束效果。

Result: 模型版本指定率6.45%-95.18%；36.70%-55.70%任务含已知CVE；62.75%-74.51%为高危/严重；72.27%-91.37%的CVE在模型知识截止前已公开；所有模型收敛于相同高风险版本；静态兼容率19.70%-63.20%；动态通过率6.49%-48.62%；外部约束可降低风险。

Conclusion: LLM版本选择是一个此前被忽视的一级风险面，存在系统性偏差而非孤立错误，外部锚定版本约束是有效的缓解策略。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are now largely involved in software development workflows, and the code they generate routinely includes third-party library (TPL) imports annotated with specific version identifiers. These version choices can carry security and compatibility risks, yet they have not been systematically studied.
  We present the first large-scale measurement study of version-level risk in LLM-generated Python code, evaluating 10 LLMs on PinTrace, a curated benchmark of 1,000 Stack Overflow programming tasks. LLMs tend to specify version identifiers when directly prompted at 26.83%-95.18%, while down to 6.45%-59.19% in creating a manifest file directly. Among the specified versions, 36.70%-55.70% of tasks contain at least one known CVE, and 62.75%-74.51% of them carry Critical or High severity ratings. In 72.27%-91.37% of cases, the associated CVEs were publicly disclosed before the model's knowledge cutoff. The statistics show all models converge on the same small set of risky release versions, indicating a systemic bias rather than isolated model error. Static compatibility rates range from 19.70% to 63.20%, with installation failure as the dominant cause. The dynamic test cases confirm the pattern by 6.49%-48.62% pass rates. Further experiments confirm that these failures are attributable to version selection rather than code quality, and that externally anchored version constraints substantially reduce both vulnerability exposure and compatibility failures. Our findings reveal LLM version selection as a first-class, previously overlooked risk surface in LLM-based development. We disclosed these findings to the community of the evaluated models, and several confirmed the issue. All the code and dataset have been released for open science at https://github.com/dw763j/PinTrace.

</details>


### [234] [Constraint Decay: The Fragility of LLM Agents in Backend Code Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06445)
*Francesco Dente,Dario Satriani,Paolo Papotti*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 系统性研究了LLM代码智能体在多文件后端生成中处理结构约束的能力，发现“约束衰减”现象：随着结构要求增加，智能体性能显著下降，在约定密集型框架中表现尤其糟糕，数据层缺陷是主要错误根源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试通常忽略结构约束（如架构模式、ORM等非功能性要求），奖励功能正确但结构随意的方案，无法反映生产级代码的实际需求。

Method: 统一API契约，在80个绿地生成任务和20个功能实现任务上，横跨8种Web框架，使用端到端行为测试和静态验证器进行双重评估。

Result: 发现约束衰减现象：强配置从基线到完全指定任务平均损失30个百分点的断言通过率，弱配置接近零；框架敏感性分析显示在Flask等简洁框架上表现好，在FastAPI、Django等约定密集型框架上表现差；数据层缺陷（错误查询组合、ORM运行时违规）是首要错误原因。

Conclusion: 同时满足功能需求和结构约束仍是编码智能体的关键开放挑战。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) agents demonstrate strong performance in autonomous code generation under loose specifications. However, production-grade software requires strict adherence to structural constraints, such as architectural patterns, databases, and object-relational mappings. Existing benchmarks often overlook these non-functional requirements, rewarding functionally correct but structurally arbitrary solutions. We present a systematic study evaluating how well agents handle structural constraints in multi-file backend generation. By fixing a unified API contract across 80 greenfield generation tasks and 20 feature-implementation tasks spanning eight web frameworks, we isolate the effect of structural complexity using a dual evaluation with end-to-end behavioral tests and static verifiers. Our findings reveal a phenomenon of constraint decay: as structural requirements accumulate, agent performance exhibits a substantial decline. Capable configurations lose 30 points on average in assertion pass rates from baseline to fully specified tasks, while some weaker configurations approach zero. Framework sensitivity analysis exposes significant performance disparities: agents succeed in minimal, explicit frameworks (e.g., Flask) but perform substantially worse on average in convention-heavy environments (e.g., FastAPI, Django). Finally, error analysis identifies data-layer defects (e.g., incorrect query composition and ORM runtime violations) as the leading root causes. This work highlights that jointly satisfying functional and structural requirements remains a key open challenge for coding agents.

</details>


### [235] [To What Extent Does Agent-generated Code Require Maintenance? An Empirical Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06464)
*Shota Sawada,Tatsuya Shirai,Yutaro Kashiwa,Ken'ichi Yamaguchi,Hiroshi Iwata,Hajimu Iida*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本研究通过分析1,000多个文件和3,200多个变更，发现AI生成代码的维护频率低于人类编写代码，AI代码的修改主要是功能扩展而非bug修复，且绝大多数维护工作由人类开发者完成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管LLM自主编码智能体在代码生成方面表现出色，但AI生成代码的长期可维护性仍存在未解问题，需要实证研究来探究其维护现状。

Method: 基于AIDev数据集（包含AI生成的PR）和GitHub，从100个流行仓库中分析了1,000+文件和约3,200个变更，对比AI生成文件与人类编写代码的维护情况。

Result: (i) AI生成文件的维护频率低于人类代码，且更新仅影响文件的一小部分；(ii) AI代码最频繁的修改是功能扩展，而人类代码的更新主要是bug修复；(iii) 绝大多数维护工作由人类开发者执行。

Conclusion: AI生成代码的维护模式与人类代码存在显著差异，当前AI代码的长期维护仍高度依赖人类开发者，提示需要改进AI编码智能体的可维护性。

Abstract: LLM-based autonomous coding agents have reshaped software development. While these agents excel at code generation, open questions persist about the long-term maintainability of AI-generated code. This study empirically investigates the maintenance extent, human involvement, and modification types of AI-generated files versus human-authored code. Using the AIDev dataset of AI-generated pull requests and GitHub, we analyzed over 1,000 files and approximately 3,200 changes from 100 popular repositories. Our findings show that: (i) AI-generated files receive less frequent maintenance than human-authored code, with updates affecting only a small fraction of file size; (ii) the most frequent modifications to AI code are feature extensions, whereas human updates focus on bug fixes, and (iii) human developers perform the large majority of this maintenance.

</details>

### [236] [Understanding Annotator Safety Policy with Interpretability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05329)
*Alex Oesterling,Donghao Ren,Yannick Assogba,Dominik Moritz,Sunnie S. Y. Kim,Leon Gatys,Fred Hohman*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出Annotator Policy Models (APMs)，通过从标注行为中学习标注者内部安全策略，无需额外标注负担即可揭示标注分歧的来源（操作失误、政策模糊性、价值多元性），并验证其在高精度建模、反事实预测和政策差异恢复上的有效性，最终应用于LLM和人类标注以支持更透明、包容的安全政策设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标注分歧普遍存在，但区分其来源（操作失误、政策模糊性、价值多元性）至关重要且困难。直接询问标注者推理过程成本高且不可靠，需要一种无需额外标注负担即可揭示标注者内部安全策略的方法。

Method: 提出Annotator Policy Models (APMs)这一可解释模型，从标注者的标签行为中学习其内部安全策略，使标注推理过程可视化和可比较，无需额外标注工作。

Result: APMs在建模标注者安全策略上达到>80%的准确率，能可靠预测反事实编辑下的响应，并在受控设置中恢复已知的政策差异。在LLM和人类标注应用中，成功揭示了政策模糊性和价值多元性。

Conclusion: APMs能够支持更有针对性、更透明和更具包容性的安全政策设计，通过揭示标注者如何不同地解释安全指令以及不同人口群体在安全优先级上的系统性差异。

Abstract: Safety policies define what constitutes safe and unsafe AI outputs, guiding data annotation and model development. However, annotation disagreement is pervasive and can stem from multiple sources such as operational failures (annotators misunderstand or misexecute the task), policy ambiguity (policy wording leaves room for interpretation), or value pluralism (different annotators hold different perspectives on safety). Distinguishing these sources matters. For example, operational failures call for quality control, ambiguity calls for policy clarification, and pluralism calls for deliberation about incorporating diverse perspectives. Yet understanding why annotators disagree is difficult. Directly asking annotators for their reasoning is costly, substantially increasing annotation burden, and can be unreliable for both human and LLM annotators as self-reported reasoning often fails to reflect actual decision processes.
  We introduce Annotator Policy Models (APMs), interpretable models that learn annotators' internal safety policies from labeling behavior alone, making annotator reasoning visible and comparable without additional annotation effort. We validate that APMs accurately model annotator safety policy (>80% accuracy), faithfully predict responses to counterfactual edits, and recover known policy differences in controlled settings. Applying APMs to LLM and human annotations, we demonstrate two core applications: (1) surfacing policy ambiguity by revealing how annotators interpret safety instructions differently, and (2) surfacing value pluralism by uncovering systematic differences in safety priorities across demographic groups. Together, these capabilities support more targeted, transparent, and inclusive safety policy design.

</details>


### [237] [ZAYA1-8B Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05365)
*Robert Washbourne,Rishi Iyer,Tomas Figliolia,Henry Zheng,Ryan Lorig-Roach,Sungyeon Yang,Pritish Yuvraj,Quentin Anthony,Yury Tokpanov,Xiao Yang,Ganesh Nanduru,Stephen Ebert,Praneeth Medepalli,Skyler Szot,Srivatsan Rajagopal,Alex Ong,Bhavana Mehta,Beren Millidge*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ZAYA1-8B是一个基于MoE++架构的推理聚焦混合专家模型，仅有7亿激活参数和80亿总参数。该模型在数学和编程基准上匹配甚至超越DeepSeek-R1-0528等大模型，并通过马尔可夫RSA测试时计算方法在AIME'25上达到91.9%准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在保持较小激活参数规模（不足10亿）的前提下，构建能够匹敌甚至超越更大规模推理模型的推理能力，并通过高效的测试时计算方法缩小与顶级大模型之间的差距。

Method: 基于Zyphra的MoE++架构构建8B总参数/700M激活参数的MoE模型；采用从预训练开始就加入推理数据的训练方案（含答案保留修剪策略）；四阶段强化学习级联：推理热身、400任务RLVE-Gym课程、数学/代码RL（含测试时计算轨迹和合成代码环境）、行为RL；提出马尔可夫RSA测试时计算方法，递归聚合并行推理轨迹，仅保留有限长度的推理尾部。

Result: ZAYA1-8B在多项数学和编程基准上匹配或超越DeepSeek-R1-0528；采用马尔可夫RSA后在AIME'25达到91.9%，在HMMT'25达到89.6%，仅需携带4K token的推理尾部，缩小了与Gemini-2.5 Pro、DeepSeek-V3.2、GPT-5-High等更大模型的差距。

Conclusion: 通过精心的架构设计、从预训练开始的推理数据注入、多阶段RL训练以及高效的测试时计算方法，小参数规模的推理模型可以达到与大规模模型竞争的性能水平，验证了MoE架构和推理优先训练策略的有效性。

Abstract: We present ZAYA1-8B, a reasoning-focused mixture-of-experts (MoE) model with 700M active and 8B total parameters, built on Zyphra's MoE++ architecture. ZAYA1-8B's core pretraining, midtraining, and supervised fine-tuning (SFT) were performed on a full-stack AMD compute, networking, and software platform. With under 1B active parameters, ZAYA1-8B matches or exceeds DeepSeek-R1-0528 on several challenging mathematics and coding benchmarks, and remains competitive with substantially larger open-weight reasoning models. ZAYA1-8B was trained from scratch for reasoning, with reasoning data included from pretraining onward using an answer-preserving trimming scheme. Post-training uses a four-stage RL cascade: reasoning warmup on math and puzzles; a 400-task RLVE-Gym curriculum; math and code RL with test-time compute traces and synthetic code environments built from competitive-programming references; and behavioral RL for chat and instruction following. We also introduce Markovian RSA, a test-time compute method that recursively aggregates parallel reasoning traces while carrying forward only bounded-length reasoning tails between rounds. In TTC evaluation, Markovian RSA raises ZAYA1-8B to 91.9\% on AIME'25 and 89.6\% on HMMT'25 while carrying forward only a 4K-token tail, narrowing the gap to much larger reasoning models including Gemini-2.5 Pro, DeepSeek-V3.2, and GPT-5-High.

</details>


### [238] [BALAR : A Bayesian Agentic Loop for Active Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05386)
*Aymen Echarghaoui,Dongxia Wu,Emily B. Fox*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: BALAR是一种无需微调的任务无关外循环算法，通过维护结构化信念、最大化期望互信息选择澄清问题，并动态扩展状态表示，在多轮交互中显著提升LLM在侦探推理、思维谜题和临床诊断三个基准上的性能（准确率提升14.6%-38.5%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大多数对话系统采用被动反应式交互，缺乏主动推理缺失信息并决定下一步提问的机制，无法有效处理需要多轮信息交换的交互式任务。

Method: BALAR是一个贝叶斯主动推理外循环算法：维护隐状态的结构化信念分布；通过最大化期望互信息选择最具有信息量的澄清问题；当当前状态表示不足时动态扩展状态空间。无需微调，即插即用。

Result: 在AR-Bench-DC（侦探案件）上准确率提升14.6%，在AR-Bench-SP（思维谜题）上提升38.5%，在iCraft-MD（临床诊断）上提升30.5%，显著优于所有基线方法。

Conclusion: BALAR通过结构化信念管理和主动信息获取策略，为LLM提供了一种高效、可泛化的多轮交互增强方案，在多个领域均表现出优越性。

Abstract: Large language models increasingly operate in interactive settings where solving a task requires multiple rounds of information exchange with a user. However, most current systems treat dialogue reactively and lack a principled mechanism to reason about what information is missing and which question should be asked next. We propose BALAR (Bayesian Agentic Loop for Active Reasoning), a task-agnostic outer-loop algorithm that requires no fine-tuning and enables structured multi-turn interaction between an LLM agent and a user. BALAR maintains a structured belief over latent states, selects clarifying questions by maximizing expected mutual information, and dynamically expands its state representation when the current one proves insufficient. We evaluate BALAR on three diverse benchmarks: AR-Bench-DC (detective cases), AR-Bench-SP (thinking puzzles), and iCraft-MD (clinical diagnosis). BALAR significantly outperforms all baselines across all three benchmarks, with $14.6\%$ higher accuracy on AR-Bench-DC, $38.5\%$ on AR-Bench-SP, and $30.5\%$ on iCraft-MD.

</details>


### [239] [Intelligent CCTV for Urban Design: AI-Based Analysis of Soft Infrastructure at Intersections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05402)
*Vinit Katariya,Seungjin Kim,Curtis Craig,Nichole Morris,Hamed Tabkhi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种基于AI的分析框架，利用现有CCTV基础设施评估软性干预措施（如临时行人避难岛和路缘扩展）对车辆速度和交通安全的影响。在明尼阿波利斯的实验表明，无信号交叉口的平均速度和85百分位速度分别下降18.75%和16.56%，通过交通量减少12.2%；信号交叉口相应降幅达20.0%和17.19%，证实了软性基础设施的交通稳静化效果及AI方法的实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统交通数据收集成本高、效率低，亟需一种快速、低成本且基于证据的方法来评估软性干预措施（如临时行人避难岛和路缘扩展）对车辆速度和交通安全的影响，以支持交通政策制定。

Method: 利用现有CCTV基础设施，结合深度学习模型和基于透视的速度估计算法，构建AI分析框架。在明尼阿波利斯选取干预地点，采集干预前、干预后第1周和第2周的视频数据，对比分析车辆速度（均值、85百分位速度）和交通量变化。

Result: 无信号交叉口：平均速度下降18.75%，85百分位速度下降16.56%，通过交通量减少12.2%。信号交叉口：除一个地点外均出现类似降幅，平均速度下降20.0%，85百分位速度下降17.19%。

Conclusion: 软性基础设施（临时行人避难岛、路缘扩展）能有效降低车辆速度、减少通过交通量，具有显著的交通稳静化效果。基于AI的分析方法可实现快速、低成本、基于证据的交通政策评估。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence (AI) and computer vision are transforming transportation data collection. This study introduces an AI-enabled analytics framework leveraging existing CCTV infrastructure to evaluate the impact of soft interventions, such as temporary pedestrian refuges and curb extensions, on vehicle speed and safety. Using deep learning and perspective-based speed estimation, we evaluated driver behavior before and after interventions, with repeated post-installation monitoring in Week 1 and Week 2, in Minneapolis. Findings reveal that at unsignalized intersections, mean and 85th-percentile speeds fell by up to 18.75% and 16.56%, respectively, while pass-through traffic decreased by as much as 12.2%. Signalized intersections showed comparable reductions except one location, with mean and 85th-percentile speeds dropping by up to 20.0% and 17.19%. These results demonstrate the traffic-calming effectiveness of soft infrastructure and underscore the utility of AI-powered methods for rapid, low-cost, and evidence-based transport policy evaluation.

### [240] [When Helpfulness Becomes Sycophancy: Sycophancy is a Boundary Failure Between Social Alignment and Epistemic Integrity in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05403)
*Jiechen Li,Catherine A. Barry,Rishika Randev,Janet Chen,Ella Jorgensen,Brinnae Bent*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文论证LLM中的谄媚现象是社会对齐与认知完整性之间的边界失效，提出一个三条件框架（用户线索、对齐行为、认知损害）及分类体系，并讨论了评估与缓解策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作将谄媚简化为外部行为（如附和不正确信念、立场反转），仅捕捉了显性形式，而未能充分界定认知完整性与社会对齐之间的微妙边界失效。

Method: 提出三条件框架：(1) 用户表达信念/偏好/自我概念的线索；(2) 模型通过对齐行为向该线索偏移；(3) 这种偏移损害了认知准确性、独立推理或适当纠正。同时引入分类体系，包括对齐目标、机制和严重程度。

Result: 给出了一个更精确的谄媚定义，将其理解为取代独立认知判断的对齐行为，而非简单的附和。提出了边界感知评估、结构化量规和缓解策略。

Conclusion: 谄媚应被视为社会对齐与认知完整性之间的边界失效，需要边界感知的评估框架来更好地理解和缓解这一问题。

Abstract: This position paper argues that sycophancy in LLMs is a boundary failure between social alignment and epistemic integrity. Existing work often operationalizes sycophancy through external behavior such as agreement with incorrect user beliefs, position reversals, or deviation from an objective standard of correctness. These formulations capture only overt forms of the phenomenon and leave subtler boundary failures involving epistemic integrity and social alignment underspecified. We argue that sycophancy should not be understood as agreement alone, but as alignment behavior that displaces independent epistemic judgment. To clarify this boundary, we propose a three-condition framework for sycophancy. First, the user expresses a cue in the form of a belief, preference, or self-concept. Second, the model shifts toward that cue through alignment behavior. Third, this shift compromises epistemic accuracy, independent reasoning, or appropriate correction. We also introduce a taxonomy for classifying sycophancy, consisting of alignment targets, mechanisms, and severity. The paper concludes by discussing implications for alignment evaluation and argues for boundary-aware assessment, structured rubrics, and mitigation strategies, while situating these proposals alongside alternative views of sycophancy.

Method: LaTA采用四阶段流水线：摄取（ingest）、分割（segment）、评分（grade）、报告（report）。使用本地托管的开源思维链LLM评分器（gpt-oss:120b），将学生作业与教师编写的参考答案进行对比，并应用带有二元逐项评分的YAML格式评分标准。
